<line act="1" scene="1" line="1" speaker="RODERIGO">Tush! never tell me; I take it much unkindly</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="2" speaker="RODERIGO">That thou, Iago, who hast had my purse</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="3" speaker="RODERIGO">As if the strings were thine, shouldst know of this.</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="4" speaker="IAGO">'Sblood, but you will not hear me:</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="5" speaker="IAGO">If ever I did dream of such a matter, Abhor me.</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="6" speaker="RODERIGO">Thou told'st me thou didst hold him in thy hate.</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="7" speaker="IAGO">Despise me, if I do not. Three great ones of the city,</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="8" speaker="IAGO">In personal suit to make me his lieutenant,</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="9" speaker="IAGO">Off-capp'd to him: and, by the faith of man,</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="10" speaker="IAGO">I know my price, I am worth no worse a place:</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="11" speaker="IAGO">But he; as loving his own pride and purposes,</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="12" speaker="IAGO">Evades them, with a bombast circumstance</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="13" speaker="IAGO">Horribly stuff'd with epithets of war;</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="14" speaker="IAGO">And, in conclusion,</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="15" speaker="IAGO">Nonsuits my mediators; for, 'Certes,' says he,</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="16" speaker="IAGO">'I have already chose my officer.'</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="17" speaker="IAGO">And what was he?</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="18" speaker="IAGO">Forsooth, a great arithmetician,</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="19" speaker="IAGO">One Michael Cassio, a Florentine,</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="20" speaker="IAGO">A fellow almost damn'd in a fair wife;</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="21" speaker="IAGO">That never set a squadron in the field,</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="22" speaker="IAGO">Nor the division of a battle knows</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="23" speaker="IAGO">More than a spinster; unless the bookish theoric,</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="24" speaker="IAGO">Wherein the toged consuls can propose</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="25" speaker="IAGO">As masterly as he: mere prattle, without practise,</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="26" speaker="IAGO">Is all his soldiership. But he, sir, had the election:</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="27" speaker="IAGO">And I, of whom his eyes had seen the proof</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="28" speaker="IAGO">At Rhodes, at Cyprus and on other grounds</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="29" speaker="IAGO">Christian and heathen, must be be-lee'd and calm'd</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="30" speaker="IAGO">By debitor and creditor: this counter-caster,</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="31" speaker="IAGO">He, in good time, must his lieutenant be,</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="32" speaker="IAGO">And I--God bless the mark!--his Moorship's ancient.</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="33" speaker="RODERIGO">By heaven, I rather would have been his hangman.</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="34" speaker="IAGO">Why, there's no remedy; 'tis the curse of service,</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="35" speaker="IAGO">Preferment goes by letter and affection,</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="36" speaker="IAGO">And not by old gradation, where each second</line><line act="1" scene="1" line="37" speaker="IAGO">Stood heir to the first. I pray you, in your letters,</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="392" speaker="OTHELLO">When you shall these unlucky deeds relate,</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="393" speaker="OTHELLO">Speak of me as I am; nothing extenuate,</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="394" speaker="OTHELLO">Nor set down aught in malice: then must you speak</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="395" speaker="OTHELLO">Of one that loved not wisely but too well;</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="396" speaker="OTHELLO">Of one not easily jealous, but being wrought</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="397" speaker="OTHELLO">Perplex'd in the extreme; of one whose hand,</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="398" speaker="OTHELLO">Like the base Indian, threw a pearl away</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="399" speaker="OTHELLO">Richer than all his tribe; of one whose subdued eyes,</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="400" speaker="OTHELLO">Albeit unused to the melting mood,</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="401" speaker="OTHELLO">Drop tears as fast as the Arabian trees</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="402" speaker="OTHELLO">Their medicinal gum. Set you down this;</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="403" speaker="OTHELLO">And say besides, that in Aleppo once,</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="404" speaker="OTHELLO">Where a malignant and a turban'd Turk</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="405" speaker="OTHELLO">Beat a Venetian and traduced the state,</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="406" speaker="OTHELLO">I took by the throat the circumcised dog,</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="407" speaker="OTHELLO">And smote him, thus.</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="408" speaker="LODOVICO">O bloody period!</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="409" speaker="GRATIANO">                  All that's spoke is marr'd.</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="410" speaker="OTHELLO">I kiss'd thee ere I kill'd thee: no way but this;</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="411" speaker="OTHELLO">Killing myself, to die upon a kiss.</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="412" speaker="CASSIO">This did I fear, but thought he had no weapon;</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="413" speaker="CASSIO">For he was great of heart.</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="414" speaker="LODOVICO">[To IAGO]  O Spartan dog,</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="415" speaker="LODOVICO">More fell than anguish, hunger, or the sea!</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="416" speaker="LODOVICO">Look on the tragic loading of this bed;</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="417" speaker="LODOVICO">This is thy work: the object poisons sight;</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="418" speaker="LODOVICO">Let it be hid. Gratiano, keep the house,</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="419" speaker="LODOVICO">And seize upon the fortunes of the Moor,</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="420" speaker="LODOVICO">For they succeed on you. To you, lord governor,</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="421" speaker="LODOVICO">Remains the censure of this hellish villain;</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="422" speaker="LODOVICO">The time, the place, the torture: O, enforce it!</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="423" speaker="LODOVICO">Myself will straight aboard: and to the state</line><line act="5" scene="2" line="424" speaker="LODOVICO">This heavy act with heavy heart relate.</line>
